37 /*
38 Client
39 Send Preface
40 Send Settings
41 Receive Settings
42 Send Settings Ack
43 Connection
44   Ping - Server Send Back Ping with Ack
45   Settings - Server Send Back Settings with Ack
46   GoAway - Connection Level Error - Attempt to send A GoAway back and disconnect noting number for replayable streams
47 
48   WindowUpdate -  Connection Level addressed to 0, each Data Frame send needs to decrease this window by the size
49                   not including the Frame header, only the content. the number of octets that the
50                   sender can transmit in addition to the existing flow-control window
51   n* Streams
52     Send WindowUpdate
53     Receive WindowUpdate
54     StreamState
55 
56     Data
57     Headers
58     Continuation
59 
60     Priority -- Has to outline something with connection
61     RstStream - Stream Level Error
62 
63     WindowUpdate
64     PushPromise - Special Case only after Open or Half-closed(remote)
65 
66  */
67 private[ember] class H2Client[F[_]: Async](
68     sg: SocketGroup[F],
69     localSettings: H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings,
70     tls: TLSContext[F],
71     connections: Ref[
72       F,
73       Map[H2Client.RequestKey, (H2Connection[F], F[Unit])],
74     ],
75     onPushPromise: (
76         org.http4s.Request[fs2.Pure],
77         F[org.http4s.Response[F]],
78     ) => F[Outcome[F, Throwable, Unit]],
79     logger: Logger[F],
80 ) {
81   import org.http4s._
82   import H2Client._
83 
84   def getOrCreate(
85       key: RequestKey,
86       useTLS: Boolean,
87       priorKnowledge: Boolean,
88   ): F[H2Connection[F]] =
89     connections.get.map(_.get(key).map(_._1)).flatMap {
90       case Some(connection) => Applicative[F].pure(connection)
91       case None =>
92         createConnection(key, useTLS, priorKnowledge).allocated.flatMap(tup =>
93           connections
94             .modify { map =>
95               val current = map.get(key)
96               val newMap = current.fold(map.+((key, tup)))(_ => map)
97               val out = current.fold(
98                 Either.left[H2Connection[F], (H2Connection[F], F[Unit])](tup._1)
99               )(r => Either.right((r._1, tup._2)))
100               (newMap, out)
101             }
102             .flatMap {
103               case Right((connection, shutdown)) =>
104                 // println("Using Reused Connection")
105                 shutdown.map(_ => connection)
106               case Left(connection) =>
107                 // println("Using Created Connection")
108                 connection.pure[F]
109             }
110         )
111     }
112 
113   //
114   def createConnection(
115       key: H2Client.RequestKey,
116       useTLS: Boolean,
117       priorKnowledge: Boolean,
118   ): Resource[F, H2Connection[F]] =
119     createSocket(key, useTLS, priorKnowledge).flatMap {
120       case (socket, Http2) => fromSocket(ByteVector.empty, socket, key)
121       case (_, Http1) => Resource.eval(InvalidSocketType().raiseError)
122     }
123 
124   // This is currently how we create http2 only sockets, will need to actually handle which
125   // protocol to take
126   def createSocket(
127       key: RequestKey,
128       useTLS: Boolean,
129       priorKnowledge: Boolean,
130   ): Resource[F, (Socket[F], SocketType)] = for {
131     address <- Resource.eval(RequestKey.getAddress(key))
132     baseSocket <- sg.client(address)
133     socket <- {
134       if (useTLS) {
135         for {
136           tlsSocket <- tls
137             .clientBuilder(baseSocket)
138             .withParameters(
139               H2TLS.transform(TLSParameters.Default)
140             )
141             .build
142           _ <- Resource.eval(tlsSocket.write(Chunk.empty))
143           protocol <- Resource.eval(H2TLS.protocol(tlsSocket))
144           socketType <- protocol match {
145             case Some("h2") => Resource.pure[F, SocketType](Http2)
146             case Some("http/1.1") => Resource.pure[F, SocketType](Http1)
147             case Some(_) =>
148               Resource.raiseError[F, SocketType, Throwable](
149                 new ProtocolException("Unknown protocol")
150               )
151             case None => Resource.pure[F, SocketType](Http1)
152           }
153         } yield (tlsSocket, socketType)
154       } else {
155         val socketType = if (priorKnowledge) Http2 else Http1
156         val out = (baseSocket, socketType)
157         Resource.pure[F, (Socket[F], SocketType)](out)
158       }
159     }
160   } yield socket
161 
162   // This Socket Becomes an Http2 Socket
163   def fromSocket(
164       acc: ByteVector,
165       socket: Socket[F],
166       key: RequestKey,
167   ): Resource[F, H2Connection[F]] =
168     for {
169       socketAdd <- Resource.eval(RequestKey.getAddress(key))
170       _ <- Resource.eval(socket.write(Chunk.byteVector(Preface.clientBV)))
171       ref <- Resource.eval(Concurrent[F].ref(Map[Int, H2Stream[F]]()))
172       initialWriteBlock <- Resource.eval(Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]])
173       stateRef <- Resource.eval(
174         Concurrent[F].ref(
175           H2Connection.State(
176             defaultSettings,
177             defaultSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize,
178             initialWriteBlock,
179             localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize,
180             0,
181             0,
182             false,
183             None,
184             None,
185           )
186         )
187       )
188       queue <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Chunk[H2Frame]]) // TODO revisit
189       hpack <- Resource.eval(Hpack.create[F])
190       settingsAck <- Resource.eval(
191         Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings]]
192       )
193       streamCreationLock <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Semaphore[F](1))
194       // data <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Frame.Data])
195       created <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Int])
196       closed <- Resource.eval(cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Int])
197       h2 = new H2Connection(
198         socketAdd.host,
199         socketAdd.port,
200         H2Connection.ConnectionType.Client,
201         localSettings,
202         ref,
203         stateRef,
204         queue,
205         created,
206         closed,
207         hpack,
208         streamCreationLock.permit,
209         settingsAck,
210         acc,
211         socket,
212         logger,
213       )
214       _ <- h2.readLoop.background
215       _ <- h2.writeLoop.compile.drain.background
216       _ <-
217         Stream
218           .fromQueueUnterminated(closed)
219           .repeat
220           .evalMap { i =>
221             if (i % 2 != 0) ref.update(m => m - i)
222             else Applicative[F].unit
223           }
224           .compile
225           .drain
226           .background
227       _ <-
228         Stream
229           .fromQueueUnterminated(created)
230           .parEvalMap(10) { i =>
231             val f = if (i % 2 == 0) {
232               val x = for {
233                 //
234                 stream <- ref.get
235                   .map(_.get(i))
236                   .flatMap(
237                     _.liftTo(new ProtocolException("Stream missing for push promise"))
238                   ) // FOLD
239                 // _ <- Sync[F].delay(println(s"Push promise stream acquired for $i"))
240                 req <- stream.getRequest
241 
242                 resp = stream.getResponse.map(
243                   _.covary[F].withBodyStream(stream.readBody)
244                 )
245                 // _ <- Sync[F].delay(println(s"Push promise request acquired for $i"))
246                 outE <- onPushPromise(req, resp).flatMap {
247                   case Outcome.Canceled() => stream.rstStream(H2Error.RefusedStream)
248                   case Outcome.Errored(_) => stream.rstStream(H2Error.RefusedStream)
249                   case Outcome.Succeeded(f) => f
250                 }.attempt
251                 _ <- ref.update(_ - i)
252                 out <- outE.liftTo[F]
253               } yield out
254               x.onError { case e => logger.warn(e)(s"Error Handling Push Promise") }.attempt.void
255             } else Applicative[F].unit
256             f
257           }
258           .compile
259           .drain
260           .onError { case e => logger.info(e)(s"Server Connection Processing Halted") } // Idle etc.
261           .background
262 
263       _ <- Resource.eval(
264         h2.outgoing.offer(
265           Chunk.singleton(H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings.toSettings(localSettings))
266         )
267       )
268       settings <- Resource.eval(h2.settingsAck.get.rethrow)
269       _ <- Resource.eval(
270         stateRef.update(s =>
271           s.copy(
272             remoteSettings = settings,
273             writeWindow = s.remoteSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize,
274           )
275         )
276       )
277     } yield h2
278 
279   def runHttp2Only(req: Request[F]): Resource[F, Response[F]] = {
280     // Host And Port are required
281     val key = H2Client.RequestKey.fromRequest(req)
282     val useTLS = req.uri.scheme.map(_.value) match {
283       case Some("http") => false
284       case Some("https") => true
285       // How Do we Choose when to use TLS, for http/1.1 this is simple its with
286       // this, but with http2, there can be arbitrary schemes
287       // but also probably wrong if doing websockets over http/1.1
288       case Some(_) => true
289       case None => true
290     }
291     val priorKnowledge = req.attributes.lookup(H2Keys.Http2PriorKnowledge).isDefined
292     val trailers = req.attributes.lookup(Message.Keys.TrailerHeaders[F])
293     for {
294       connection <- Resource.eval(getOrCreate(key, useTLS, priorKnowledge))
295       // Stream Order Must Be Correct, so we must grab the global lock
296       stream <- Resource.make(
297         connection.streamCreateAndHeaders.use(_ =>
298           connection.initiateLocalStream.flatMap(stream =>
299             stream.sendHeaders(PseudoHeaders.requestToHeaders(req), false).as(stream)
300           )
301         )
302       )(stream => connection.mapRef.update(m => m - stream.id))
303       _ <- (req.body.chunks.noneTerminate.zipWithNext
304         .evalMap {
305           case (Some(c), Some(Some(_))) => stream.sendData(c.toByteVector, false)
306           case (Some(c), Some(None) | None) =>
307             if (trailers.isDefined) stream.sendData(c.toByteVector, false)
308             else stream.sendData(c.toByteVector, true)
309           case (None, _) =>
310             if (trailers.isDefined) Applicative[F].unit
311             else stream.sendData(ByteVector.empty, true)
312         }
313         .compile
314         .drain >> trailers.sequence.flatMap(optTrailers =>
315         optTrailers
316           .flatMap(h => h.headers.map(a => (a.name.toString.toLowerCase(), a.value, false)).toNel)
317           .traverse(nel => stream.sendHeaders(nel, true))
318       )).background
319       resp <- Resource.eval(stream.getResponse).map(_.covary[F].withBodyStream(stream.readBody))
320     } yield resp
321   }
322 }
323 
324 private[ember] object H2Client {
325   private type TinyClient[F[_]] = Request[F] => Resource[F, Response[F]]
326   def impl[F[_]: Async](
327       onPushPromise: (
328           org.http4s.Request[fs2.Pure],
329           F[org.http4s.Response[F]],
330       ) => F[Outcome[F, Throwable, Unit]],
331       tlsContext: TLSContext[F],
332       logger: Logger[F],
333       settings: H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings = defaultSettings,
334   ): Resource[F, TinyClient[F] => TinyClient[F]] =
335     for {
336 
337       mapH2 <- Resource.make {
338         Concurrent[F].ref(
339           Map[H2Client.RequestKey, (H2Connection[F], F[Unit])]()
340         )
341       } { ref =>
342         ref.get.flatMap(_.toList.traverse_ { case (_, (_, s)) => s }.attempt.void)
343       }
344       socketMap <- Resource.eval(
345         Concurrent[F].ref(Map[H2Client.RequestKey, SocketType]())
346       )
347 
348       _ <- Stream
349         .awakeDelay(1.seconds)
350         .evalMap(_ => mapH2.get)
351         .flatMap(m => Stream.emits(m.toList))
352         .evalMap { case (t, (connection, shutdown)) =>
353           connection.state.get.flatMap { s =>
354             if (s.closed) mapH2.update(m => m - t) >> shutdown else Applicative[F].unit
355           }.attempt
356         }
357         .compile
358         .drain
359         .background
360       h2 = new H2Client(Network[F], settings, tlsContext, mapH2, onPushPromise, logger)
361     } yield (http1Client: TinyClient[F]) => { (req: Request[F]) =>
362       val key = H2Client.RequestKey.fromRequest(req)
363       val priorKnowledge = req.attributes.lookup(H2Keys.Http2PriorKnowledge).isDefined
364       val socketTypeF = if (priorKnowledge) Some(Http2).pure[F] else socketMap.get.map(_.get(key))
365       Resource.eval(socketTypeF).flatMap {
366         case Some(Http2) => h2.runHttp2Only(req)
367         case Some(Http1) => http1Client(req)
368         case None =>
369           (
370             h2.runHttp2Only(req) <*
371               Resource.eval(socketMap.update(s => s + (key -> Http2)))
372           ).handleErrorWith[org.http4s.Response[F], Throwable] {
373             case InvalidSocketType() | MissingHost() | MissingPort() =>
374               Resource.eval(socketMap.update(s => s + (key -> Http1))) >>
375                 http1Client(req)
376             case e => Resource.raiseError[F, Response[F], Throwable](e)
377           }
378       }
379     }
380 
381   sealed trait SocketType extends Product with Serializable
382   case object Http2 extends SocketType
383   case object Http1 extends SocketType
384 
385   /** Represents a key for requests that can conceivably share a [[Connection]]. */
386   final case class RequestKey(scheme: Scheme, authority: Authority) {
387     override def toString: String = s"${scheme.value}://${authority}"
388   }
389 
390   object RequestKey {
391     def fromRequest[F[_]](request: Request[F]): RequestKey = {
392       val uri = request.uri
393       RequestKey(uri.scheme.getOrElse(Scheme.http), uri.authority.getOrElse(Authority()))
394     }
395 
396     def getAddress[F[_]: Sync](requestKey: RequestKey): F[SocketAddress[Host]] =
397       requestKey match {
398         case RequestKey(s, auth) =>
399           val port = auth.port.getOrElse(if (s == Uri.Scheme.https) 443 else 80)
400           val host = auth.host.value
401           for {
402             host <- Host.fromString(host).liftTo[F](MissingHost())
403             port <- Port.fromInt(port).liftTo[F](MissingPort())
404           } yield SocketAddress[Host](host, port)
405       }
406   }
407 
408   private[h2] case class InvalidSocketType()
409       extends RuntimeException("createConnection only supports http2, and this is not available")
410 
411   private case class MissingHost() extends RuntimeException("Hostname missing")
412 
413   private case class MissingPort() extends RuntimeException("Port missing")
414 }
